摘要：AI 應用程序正逐漸被引入數位健康領域。<lb/>儘管技術性能迅速進步，但成功的部署主要依賴於消費者的態度，特別是對面向患者的應用程序。<lb/>然而，大多數現有研究是在抽象層面上檢視消費者對醫療保健 AI 的態度，而不是針對具體的實物。<lb/>我們報告了一項在澳大利亞進行的混合方法調查研究（N=275），檢視消費者對醫療保健 AI 的準備程度、接受度、信任和風險感知，並結合了基於情境的評估，評估 AI 生成的諮詢摘要與臨床醫生撰寫的摘要。<lb/>參與者表達了中等的樂觀情緒和強烈的感知有用性及易用性，但也對準確性、安全性和數據使用表達了相當大的擔憂。<lb/>在情境任務中，AI 生成的摘要在質量、同理心和整體有用性方面被強烈偏好，但對 AI 摘要的識別接近隨機。<lb/>研究結果顯示，消費者通過具體的溝通質量和可見的人類治理來評判 AI，強調了除了技術性能之外，臨床監督的部署框架的必要性。

##### **Iterative Multimodal Retrieval-Augmented Generation for Medical Question Answering**
2604.27724v1 by Xupeng Chen, Binbin Shi, Chenqian Le, Jiaqi Zhang, Kewen Wang, Ran Gong, Jinhan Zhang, Chihang Wang

Medical retrieval-augmented generation (RAG) systems typically operate on text chunks extracted from biomedical literature, discarding the rich visual content (tables, figures, structured layouts) of original document pages. We propose MED-VRAG, an iterative multimodal RAG framework that retrieves and reasons over PMC document page images instead of OCR'd text. The system pairs ColQwen2.5 patch-level page embeddings with a sharded MapReduce LLM filter, scaling to ~350K pages while keeping Stage-1 retrieval under 30 ms via an offline coarse-to-fine index (C=8 centroids per page, ANN over centroids, exact two-way scoring on the top-R shortlist). A vision-language model (VLM) then iteratively refines its query and accumulates evidence in a memory bank across up to 3 reasoning rounds, with a single iteration costing ~15.9 s and the full three-round pipeline ~47.8 s on 4xA100. Across four medical QA benchmarks (MedQA, MedMCQA, PubMedQA, MMLU-Med), MEDVRAG reaches 78.6% average accuracy. Under controlled comparison with the same Qwen2.5-VL-32B backbone, retrieval contributes a +5.8 point gain over the no-retrieval baseline; we also note a +1.8 point edge over MedRAG + GPT-4 (76.8%), with the caveat that this is a cross-paper rather than head-to-head comparison. Ablations isolate +1.0 from page-image vs text-chunk retrieval, +1.5 from iteration, and +1.0 from the memory bank.

摘要：醫療檢索增強生成（RAG）系統通常基於從生物醫學文獻中提取的文本片段運作，忽略了原始文檔頁面中的豐富視覺內容（表格、圖形、結構化佈局）。我們提出了MED-VRAG，一種迭代的多模態RAG框架，它檢索並推理PMC文檔頁面圖像，而不是OCR文本。該系統將ColQwen2.5的補丁級頁面嵌入與分片的MapReduce LLM過濾器配對，擴展到約350K頁，同時通過離線的粗到細索引保持第一階段檢索在30毫秒以內（每頁8個質心，對質心進行ANN，對前R短列表進行精確的雙向打分）。然後，視覺-語言模型（VLM）在最多3輪推理中迭代地細化其查詢並在記憶庫中累積證據，單次迭代約需15.9秒，完整的三輪管道在4xA100上約需47.8秒。在四個醫療問答基準（MedQA、MedMCQA、PubMedQA、MMLU-Med）中，MED-VRAG達到78.6%的平均準確率。在與相同Qwen2.5-VL-32B骨幹的受控比較中，檢索相較於無檢索基準貢獻了+5.8的增益；我們還注意到相較於MedRAG + GPT-4（76.8%）有+1.8的優勢，但需要注意的是這是一個跨論文而非正面比較。消融實驗顯示，頁面圖像與文本片段檢索之間的增益為+1.0，迭代的增益為+1.5，記憶庫的增益為+1.0。

##### **Auditing Frontier Vision-Language Models for Trustworthy Medical VQA: Grounding Failures, Format Collapse, and Domain Adaptation**
2604.27720v1 by Xupeng Chen, Binbin Shi, Chenqian Le, Qifu Yin, Lang Lin, Haowei Ni, Ran Gong, Panfeng Li

Deploying vision-language models (VLMs) in clinical settings demands auditable behavior under realistic failure conditions, yet the failure landscape of frontier VLMs on specialized medical inputs is poorly characterized. We audit five recent frontier and grounding-aware VLMs (Gemini~2.5~Pro, GPT-5, o3, GLM-4.5V, Qwen~2.5~VL) on Medical VQA along two trust-relevant axes. Perception: all models localize anatomical and pathological targets poorly -- the best model reaches only 0.23 mean IoU and 19.1% Acc@0.5 -- and exhibit clinically dangerous laterality confusion. Pipeline integration: a self-grounding pipeline, where the same model localizes then answers, degrades VQA accuracy for every model -- driven by both inaccurate localization and format-compliance failures under the two-step prompt (parse failure rises to 70%--99% for Gemini and GPT-5 on VQA-RAD). Replacing predicted boxes with ground-truth annotations recovers and improves VQA accuracy, consistent with the failure residing in the perception module rather than in the decomposition itself. These observational findings identify grounding quality as a primary trustworthiness bottleneck in our SLAKE bounding-box setting. As a complementary fine-tuning follow-up, supervised fine-tuning of Qwen~2.5~VL on combined Med-VQA training data attains the highest reported SLAKE open-ended recall (85.5%) among comparable methods, suggesting that the VQA-level gap is tractable with domain adaptation; whether this also closes the perception/trustworthiness bottleneck is left to future work.

摘要：在臨床環境中部署視覺-語言模型 (VLMs) 需要在現實失敗條件下具備可審計的行為，但前沿 VLMs 在專門醫療輸入上的失敗情況尚未得到充分描述。我們對五個最近的前沿和具備基礎知識的 VLMs（Gemini~2.5~Pro、GPT-5、o3、GLM-4.5V、Qwen~2.5~VL）在醫療 VQA 上進行了審計，並沿著兩個與信任相關的軸進行評估。感知：所有模型在定位解剖和病理目標方面表現不佳——最佳模型僅達到 0.23 的平均 IoU 和 19.1% 的 Acc@0.5——並且表現出臨床上危險的側向混淆。管道整合：一個自我基礎的管道，其中同一模型先定位再回答，對每個模型的 VQA 準確性造成了下降——這是由於在兩步提示下的定位不準確和格式合規失敗（對於 VQA-RAD，Gemini 和 GPT-5 的解析失敗率上升至 70%--99%）。用真實標註替換預測框可以恢復並改善 VQA 準確性，這與失敗存在於感知模組而非分解本身是一致的。這些觀察結果確定了基礎質量作為我們 SLAKE 邊界框設置中的主要信任瓶頸。作為補充的微調後續，對 Qwen~2.5~VL 在結合的 Med-VQA 訓練數據上進行的監督微調，在可比較的方法中達到了最高報告的 SLAKE 開放式召回率 (85.5%)，這表明 VQA 層級的差距可以通過領域適應來解決；是否這也能關閉感知/信任瓶頸則留待未來的工作。

##### **Deep Learning-Based Segmentation of Peritoneal Cancer Index Regions from CT Imaging**
2604.27697v1 by Pieter C. Gort, Lotte J. S. Ewals, Marion W. Tops-Welten, Cris H. B. Claessens, Joost Nederend, Fons van der Sommen

Peritoneal metastases are currently assessed using diagnostic laparoscopy to determine Sugarbaker's Peritoneal Cancer Index (sPCI), which works by dividing the abdomen into 13 regions and scoring each region based on tumor size. A recent consensus study defined 3D regions to facilitate a radiological PCI (rPCI), providing standardized anatomical regions for imaging-based assessment. Despite its clinical value, sPCI is invasive and lacks a standardized imaging counterpart. In this study, we propose a deep learning-based approach to automatically segment the rPCI regions on CT. We evaluate nnU-Net and Swin UNETR on 62 CT scans with rPCI regions manually annotated by three clinical researchers and validated by two expert radiologists. Performance was assessed using five-fold cross-validation with the Dice Similarity Coefficient (Dice), 95th percentile Hausdorff distance and Average Surface Distance. nnU-Net achieved an overall Dice of 0.82, approaching interobserver agreement (0.88) and outperforming Swin UNETR (0.76), with remaining challenges primarily in right flank and small-bowel regions. These results demonstrate feasibility of automated rPCI segmentation, laying the foundation for non-invasive, imaging-based assessment.

摘要：腹膜轉移目前使用診斷性腹腔鏡檢查來評估 Sugarbaker 的腹膜癌指數 (sPCI)，該指數通過將腹部劃分為 13 個區域並根據腫瘤大小對每個區域進行打分來運作。最近的一項共識研究定義了 3D 區域，以促進放射學 PCI (rPCI)，為基於影像的評估提供標準化的解剖區域。儘管 sPCI 具有臨床價值，但它是侵入性的，並且缺乏標準化的影像對應物。在這項研究中，我們提出了一種基於深度學習的方法，自動分割 CT 上的 rPCI 區域。我們在 62 例 CT 掃描上評估了 nnU-Net 和 Swin UNETR，這些掃描的 rPCI 區域由三位臨床研究人員手動標註，並由兩位專家放射科醫生驗證。性能評估使用了五折交叉驗證，並計算了 Dice 相似度係數 (Dice)、第 95 百分位的 Hausdorff 距離和平均表面距離。nnU-Net 的 Dice 總體達到 0.82，接近觀察者間一致性 (0.88)，並且優於 Swin UNETR (0.76)，剩餘的挑戰主要集中在右側腹部和小腸區域。這些結果顯示了自動化 rPCI 分割的可行性，為非侵入性、基於影像的評估奠定了基礎。

##### **Robust Lightweight Crack Classification for Real-Time UAV Bridge Inspection**
2604.27617v1 by Wei Li, Haisheng Li, Weijie Li, Jiandong Wang, Kaichen Ma, Luming Yang

With the widespread application of Unmanned Aerial Vehicles (UAVs) in bridge structural health monitoring, deep learning-based automatic crack detection has become a major research focus. However, practical UAV inspections still face four key challenges: weak crack features, degraded imaging conditions, severe class imbalance, and limited computational resources for practical UAV inspection workflows. To address these issues, this paper proposes a unified lightweight convolutional neural network framework composed of four synergistic components: a lightweight backbone network, a Convolutional Block Attention Module (CBAM) for channel and spatial enhancement, a directed robust augmentation strategy based on inspection-scene priors, and Focal Loss for hard-sample learning under class imbalance. Experiments on the SDNET2018 bridge deck dataset show that the proposed method achieves an inference speed of 825 FPS with only 11.21M parameters and 1.82G FLOPs. Compared with the baseline model, the complete framework improves the F1-score by 2.51% and recall by 3.95%. In addition, Grad-CAM visualizations indicate that the introduced attention module shifts the model's focus from scattered regions to precise tracking along crack trajectories. Overall, this study achieves a strong balance among accuracy, speed, and robustness, providing a practical solution for ground-station assisted real-time deployment in UAV bridge inspections. The source code is available at: https://github.com/skylynf/AttXNet .

摘要：隨著無人機（UAV）在橋樑結構健康監測中的廣泛應用，基於深度學習的自動裂縫檢測已成為主要的研究焦點。<lb/>然而，實際的無人機檢查仍面臨四個關鍵挑戰：裂縫特徵薄弱、成像條件惡化、類別不平衡嚴重，以及實際無人機檢查工作流程中計算資源有限。<lb/>為了解決這些問題，本文提出了一個統一的輕量級卷積神經網絡框架，由四個協同組件組成：一個輕量級的主幹網絡、一個用於通道和空間增強的卷積塊注意力模塊（CBAM）、一個基於檢查場景先驗的有向穩健增強策略，以及用於類別不平衡下難樣本學習的焦點損失（Focal Loss）。<lb/>在SDNET2018橋面數據集上的實驗表明，所提出的方法在僅有11.21M參數和1.82G FLOPs的情況下達到了825 FPS的推理速度。<lb/>與基線模型相比，完整框架將F1-score提高了2.51%，召回率提高了3.95%。<lb/>此外，Grad-CAM可視化結果顯示，引入的注意力模塊將模型的重點從分散區域轉移到沿裂縫軌跡的精確跟踪。<lb/>總體而言，本研究在準確性、速度和穩健性之間實現了良好的平衡，為無人機橋樑檢查中的地面站輔助實時部署提供了實用解決方案。<lb/>源代碼可在以下鏈接獲得：https://github.com/skylynf/AttXNet 。

##### **RIHA: Report-Image Hierarchical Alignment for Radiology Report Generation**
2604.27559v1 by Yucheng Chen, Yang Yu, Yufei Shi, Conghao Xiong, Xulei Yang, Si Yong Yeo

Radiology report generation (RRG) has emerged as a promising approach to alleviate radiologists' workload and reduce human errors by automatically generating diagnostic reports from medical images. A key challenge in RRG is achieving fine-grained alignment between complex visual features and the hierarchical structure of long-form radiology reports. Although recent methods have improved image-text representation learning, they often treat reports as flat sequences, overlooking their structured sections and semantic hierarchies. This simplification hinders precise cross-modal alignment and weakens RRG accuracy. To address this challenge, we propose RIHA (Report-Image Hierarchical Alignment Transformer), a novel end-to-end framework that performs multi-level alignment between radiological images and their corresponding reports across paragraph, sentence, and word levels. This hierarchical alignment enables more precise cross-modal mapping, essential for capturing the nuanced semantics embedded in clinical narratives. Specifically, RIHA introduces a Visual Feature Pyramid (VFP) to extract multi-scale visual features and a Text Feature Pyramid (TFP) to represent multi-granularity textual structures. These components are integrated through a Cross-modal Hierarchical Alignment (CHA) module, leveraging optimal transport to effectively align visual and textual features across various levels. Furthermore, we incorporate Relative Positional Encoding (RPE) into the decoder to model spatial and semantic relationships among tokens, enhancing the token-level alignment between visual features and generated text. Extensive experiments on two benchmark chest X-ray datasets, IU-Xray and MIMIC-CXR, demonstrate that RIHA outperforms existing state-of-the-art models in both natural language generation and clinical efficacy metrics.

摘要：放射學報告生成（RRG）已成為一種有前景的方法，旨在減輕放射科醫生的工作負擔並通過自動從醫學影像生成診斷報告來減少人為錯誤。<lb/>RRG的一個主要挑戰是實現複雜視覺特徵與長格式放射學報告的層次結構之間的細緻對齊。<lb/>儘管最近的方法改善了圖像-文本表示學習，但它們通常將報告視為平坦序列，忽略了其結構化的部分和語義層次。<lb/>這種簡化妨礙了精確的跨模態對齊，並削弱了RRG的準確性。<lb/>為了解決這一挑戰，我們提出了RIHA（報告-影像層次對齊Transformer），這是一個新穎的端到端框架，能夠在段落、句子和單詞層面上對放射影像及其相應報告進行多層次對齊。<lb/>這種層次對齊使得更精確的跨模態映射成為可能，這對於捕捉臨床敘事中嵌入的細微語義至關重要。<lb/>具體來說，RIHA引入了一個視覺特徵金字塔（VFP）來提取多尺度視覺特徵，以及一個文本特徵金字塔（TFP）來表示多粒度文本結構。<lb/>這些組件通過一個跨模態層次對齊（CHA）模塊集成，利用最佳運輸有效地對齊各個層次的視覺和文本特徵。<lb/>此外，我們在解碼器中納入了相對位置編碼（RPE），以建模標記之間的空間和語義關係，增強視覺特徵與生成文本之間的標記級對齊。<lb/>在兩個基準胸部X光數據集IU-Xray和MIMIC-CXR上的廣泛實驗表明，RIHA在自然語言生成和臨床效能指標上均超越了現有的最先進模型。

##### **Beyond the Mean: Within-Model Reliable Change Detection for LLM Evaluation**
2604.27405v1 by Jon-Paul Cacioli

We adapted the Reliable Change Index (RCI; Jacobson and Truax, 1991) from clinical psychology to item-level LLM version comparison on 2,000 MMLU-Pro items (K=10 samples at T=0.7). Two within-family pairs were tested: Llama 3 to 3.1 (+1.6 points) and Qwen 2.5 to 3 (+2.8 points). On the full benchmark, most items showed no reliable change (79% and 72%). However, over half the items were floor/ceiling. Among analysable items, change was bidirectional with large effect sizes: 34% improved and 28% deteriorated for Llama; 47% improved and 39% deteriorated for Qwen (median |delta p| = 0.50 and 0.90). Churn was asymmetric by difficulty: low-accuracy items improved, high-accuracy items deteriorated. Domain-level decomposition revealed family-specific reversals: Llama lost physics while Qwen lost law. Greedy single-shot evaluation missed 42% of reliably changed items and falsely flagged 25% of unchanged items. The aggregate accuracy gain is the net residual of opposing item-level movements. We recommend reporting churn rate alongside aggregate accuracy.

摘要：我們將可靠變化指數（RCI；Jacobson 和 Truax，1991）從臨床心理學適應到 2,000 個 MMLU-Pro 項目的項目級 LLM 版本比較（K=10 取樣於 T=0.7）。測試了兩對同一家族的模型：Llama 3 到 3.1（+1.6 分）和 Qwen 2.5 到 3（+2.8 分）。在完整基準中，大多數項目顯示沒有可靠變化（79% 和 72%）。然而，超過一半的項目為底部/頂部效應。在可分析的項目中，變化是雙向的，且效果大小很大：Llama 有 34% 改進和 28% 惡化；Qwen 則有 47% 改進和 39% 惡化（中位數 |delta p| = 0.50 和 0.90）。變化在難度上是不對稱的：低準確度的項目改善，高準確度的項目惡化。領域級分解顯示出特定於家族的逆轉：Llama 在物理學上失分，而 Qwen 在法律上失分。貪婪的單次評估錯過了 42% 的可靠變化項目，並錯誤標記了 25% 的未變化項目。總體準確度增益是相對於項目級變動的淨殘差。我們建議在報告總體準確度的同時報告變化率。

##### **Safe Bilevel Delegation (SBD): A Formal Framework for Runtime Delegation Safety in Multi-Agent Systems**
2604.27358v1 by Yuan Sun

As large language model (LLM) agents are deployed in high-stakes environments, the question of how safely to delegate subtasks to specialized sub-agents becomes critical. Existing work addresses multi-agent architecture selection at design time or provides broad empirical guidelines, but neither provides a runtime mechanism that dynamically adjusts the safety-efficiency trade-off as task context changes during execution.
  We propose Safe Bilevel Delegation (SBD), a formal framework for runtime delegation safety in hierarchical multi-agent systems. SBD formulates task delegation as a bilevel optimization problem: an outer meta-weight network phi learns context-dependent safety-efficiency weights lambda(s) in [0,1]; an inner loop optimizes the delegation policy pi subject to a probabilistic safety constraint P(safe) >= 1-delta. The continuous delegation degree alpha in [0, 1] controls how much decision authority is transferred to each sub-agent, interpolating smoothly between full human override (alpha=0) and fully autonomous execution (alpha=1).
  We establish three theoretical results: (1) Safety Monotonicity--higher outer safety weight produces a weakly safer inner policy; (2) Inner Policy Convergence--projected gradient descent on the inner problem converges linearly under standard smoothness assumptions; (3) an Accountability Propagation bound that distributes responsibility across multi-hop delegation chains with a provable per-agent ceiling. We instantiate SBD in three high-stakes domains--medical AI (MIMIC-III), financial risk control (S and P 500), and educational agent supervision (ASSISTments)--specifying datasets, safety constraint sets, baselines, and evaluation protocols. This manuscript presents the formal framework and theoretical results in full; empirical validation following the protocols described herein is planned and will be reported in a forthcoming revision.

摘要：隨著大型語言模型（LLM）代理在高風險環境中的部署，如何安全地將子任務委派給專門的子代理的問題變得至關重要。現有的研究在設計階段處理多代理架構的選擇或提供廣泛的實證指導，但都未提供一種在執行過程中隨著任務上下文變化而動態調整安全性與效率權衡的運行時機制。<lb/>  
我們提出了安全雙層委派（Safe Bilevel Delegation, SBD），這是一個用於層級多代理系統的運行時委派安全的正式框架。SBD將任務委派公式化為一個雙層優化問題：外部元權重網路phi學習上下文依賴的安全效率權重lambda(s)在[0,1]之間；內部循環在概率安全約束P(safe) >= 1-delta的條件下優化委派策略pi。連續的委派程度alpha在[0, 1]之間控制著轉移給每個子代理的決策權限，平滑地插值於完全人類覆蓋（alpha=0）和完全自主執行（alpha=1）之間。<lb/>  
我們建立了三個理論結果：（1）安全單調性——更高的外部安全權重產生一個弱安全的內部策略；（2）內部政策收斂——在標準光滑性假設下，內部問題的投影梯度下降以線性速度收斂；（3）一個責任傳播界限，將責任分配到多跳委派鏈中，並具有可證的每代理上限。我們在三個高風險領域實現了SBD——醫療AI（MIMIC-III）、金融風險控制（S and P 500）和教育代理監督（ASSISTments）——具體說明了數據集、安全約束集、基準和評估協議。本文完整地呈現了正式框架和理論結果；根據此處描述的協議進行的實證驗證計劃將在即將到來的修訂中報告。

##### **End-to-End Evaluation and Governance of an EHR-Embedded AI Agent for Clinicians**
2604.27309v1 by Aaryan Shah, Andrew Hines, Alexia Downs, Denis Bajet, Paulius Mui, Fabiano Araujo, Laura Offutt, Aida Rutledge, Elizabeth Jimenez

Clinical AI systems require not just point-in-time evaluation but continuous governance: the ongoing practice of monitoring, evaluating, iterating, and re-evaluating performance throughout deployment. We present an end-to-end framework of governance that integrates rubric validation, live deployment feedback, technical performance monitoring, and cost tracking, with controlled experimentation gating system changes before deployment. Applied to Hyperscribe, an EHR-embedded agent that converts ambient audio into structured chart updates, twenty clinicians authored 1,646 validated rubrics across 823 cases. Seven Hyperscribe versions were evaluated through controlled experiments, with median scores improving from 84% to 95%. Analysis of 107 live feedback entries over three months showed feedback composition shifting from 79% error reports and 14% positive observations to 30% errors and 45% positive observations as engineering interventions resolved failures. Median processing time per audio segment was 8.1 seconds with a 99.6% effective completion rate after retry mechanisms absorbed transient model errors. These results demonstrate that continuous, multi-channel governance of deployed clinical AI is both achievable and effective.

摘要：臨床 AI 系統不僅需要即時評估，還需要持續的治理：在部署過程中持續監控、評估、迭代和重新評估性能的實踐。我們提出了一個端到端的治理框架，該框架整合了標準驗證、實時部署反饋、技術性能監控和成本追蹤，並在部署之前通過受控實驗來控制系統變更。應用於 Hyperscribe，一個將環境音頻轉換為結構化病歷更新的 EHR 嵌入式代理，二十位臨床醫生在 823 個案例中撰寫了 1,646 個經過驗證的標準。七個 Hyperscribe 版本通過受控實驗進行評估，中位數分數從 84% 提高到 95%。對三個月內 107 條實時反饋條目的分析顯示，反饋組成從 79% 的錯誤報告和 14% 的正面觀察轉變為 30% 的錯誤和 45% 的正面觀察，因為工程干預解決了故障。每段音頻的中位處理時間為 8.1 秒，經過重試機制吸收瞬態模型錯誤後，完成率達到 99.6%。這些結果表明，對已部署的臨床 AI 進行持續的多渠道治理既可實現又有效。
